[31m+ // Uncapped for levelsetting — log attempts but don't limit[39m
[31m+ export const MAX_COMPILE_ATTEMPTS = 20[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Persist a routing_card session message that links the just-completed[39m
[31m+  * route_plan to its session so the map can render it. The orchestrator runs[39m
[31m+  * planRoute inside a sub-agent whose tool loop doesn't fire the parent[39m
[31m+  * onToolFinish callback, so without this the route_plan is orphaned (created in[39m
[31m+  * the route_plans table but never linked to a session_message for display).[39m
[31m+  * Mirrors the card logic in sendMessage.ts onToolFinish. (FIX-001 display.)[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ async function persistRoutingCard(ctx: AgentContext, routePlanId: Id<'route_plans'>) {[39m
[31m+   const { messageId } = await ctx.runMutation([39m
[31m+     internal.db.sessionMessages.createPendingAssistantMessage,[39m
[31m+     {[39m
[31m+       sessionId: ctx.planningSessionId,[39m
[31m+       kind: 'routing_card',[39m
[31m+       attachments: [{ type: 'route_options', routePlanId }],[39m
[31m+     },[39m
[31m+   )[39m
[31m+   await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.sessionMessages.finalizeAssistantMessage, {[39m
[31m+     messageId,[39m
[31m+     status: 'complete',[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // In-Memory Sketch Store (per-session)[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // Session-scoped state for sketch compilation — tracks pending sketches, succeeded[39m
[31m+ // segment cache, and attempt count for the retry loop.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ type SegmentIdentity = {[39m
[31m+   roadName: string[39m
[31m+   fromName: string[39m
[31m+   toName: string[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ type CachedSegmentResult = {[39m
[31m+   // The original segment index in the sketch passed to the first compileSketch call[39m
[31m+   segmentIndex: number[39m
[31m+   route: import('../providers/routingProvider').ProviderRouteResponse[39m
[31m+   identity: SegmentIdentity[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ type PendingSketchState = {[39m
[31m+   sketch: any[39m
[31m+   succeededSegments: CachedSegmentResult[][39m
[31m+   attemptCount: number[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ const pendingSketches = new Map<string, PendingSketchState>()[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export function storePendingSketch(sessionId: string, sketch: any): void {[39m
[31m+   // Reset the sketch state when a new sketch is stored (LLM called createRouteSketch again)[39m
[31m+   pendingSketches.set(sessionId, { sketch, succeededSegments: [], attemptCount: 0 })[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export function getPendingSketchState(sessionId: string): PendingSketchState | undefined {[39m
[31m+   return pendingSketches.get(sessionId)[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export function updatePendingSketchState(sessionId: string, state: PendingSketchState): void {[39m
[31m+   pendingSketches.set(sessionId, state)[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export function clearPendingSketch(sessionId: string): void {[39m
[31m+   pendingSketches.delete(sessionId)[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // Legacy accessor — kept for createRouteSketch handler which only needs the sketch[39m
[31m+ export function getPendingSketch(sessionId: string): any | undefined {[39m
[31m+   return pendingSketches.get(sessionId)?.sketch[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Segment identity key for change detection.[39m
[31m+  * Two segments with the same (roadName, fromName, toName) are considered identical.[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export function segmentKey(seg: SegmentIdentity): string {[39m
[31m+   return `${seg.roadName}||${seg.fromName}||${seg.toName}`[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Find which segments in the new sketch are unchanged compared to previously-succeeded segments.[39m
[31m+  * Returns a map from new-sketch-index → cached result for each unchanged segment.[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export function findUnchangedSegments([39m
[31m+   newSegments: SegmentIdentity[],[39m
[31m+   cached: CachedSegmentResult[],[39m
[31m+ ): Map<number, CachedSegmentResult> {[39m
[31m+   const cachedByKey = new Map(cached.map((r) => [segmentKey(r.identity), r]))[39m
[31m+   const unchanged = new Map<number, CachedSegmentResult>()[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   newSegments.forEach((seg, idx) => {[39m
[31m+     const hit = cachedByKey.get(segmentKey(seg))[39m
[31m+     if (hit) {[39m
[31m+       unchanged.set(idx, hit)[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   return unchanged[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Merge cached succeeded segments with newly-compiled results into a single ordered array.[39m
[31m+  * The result is ordered by segmentIndex (position in the new sketch).[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export function mergeSegmentResults([39m
[31m+   newSegments: SegmentIdentity[],[39m
[31m+   unchanged: Map<number, CachedSegmentResult>,[39m
[31m+   newResults: import('../tools/compileSketch').SegmentCompileResult[],[39m
[31m+ ): import('../tools/compileSketch').SegmentCompileResult[] {[39m
[31m+   // newResults are indexed relative to the toCompile subset — remap them[39m
[31m+   // The compile call was given segments in order; map back to sketch index[39m
[31m+   let newResultIdx = 0[39m
[31m+   const merged: import('../tools/compileSketch').SegmentCompileResult[] = [][39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   for (let i = 0; i < newSegments.length; i++) {[39m
[31m+     const cached = unchanged.get(i)[39m
[31m+     if (cached) {[39m
[31m+       merged.push({ status: 'ok', segmentIndex: i, route: cached.route })[39m
[31m+     } else {[39m
[31m+       // This was a segment we compiled — get from newResults in order[39m
[31m+       const r = newResults[newResultIdx++][39m
[31m+       if (r) {[39m
[31m+         merged.push({ ...r, segmentIndex: i })[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   return merged[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // Tool Handlers[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Geocode a place name to coordinates.[39m
[31m+  * Exported for reuse by searchAgent (US-078).[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export async function runGeocode(ctx: AgentContext, args: { query: string }): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   const provider = createGeocodingProvider()[39m
[31m+   const results = await provider.geocode(args.query, ctx.currentLocation)[39m
[31m+   if (results.length === 0) {[39m
[31m+     return {[39m
[31m+       type: 'error',[39m
[31m+       message: `No results found for "${args.query}"`,[39m
[31m+       hint: 'Try a more specific query with city/state, e.g. "Santa Cruz, CA" instead of "Santa Cruz"',[39m
[31m+       retryGuidance: 'different_args',[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+   return { results: results.slice(0, 3) }[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ async function _runLookupRoad([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+   args: {[39m
[31m+     roadName: string[39m
[31m+     bbox: { south: number; west: number; north: number; east: number }[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   // Try Convex OSM data first for fast name lookup[39m
[31m+   try {[39m
[31m+     const ways = await ctx.runAction(internal.actions.osm.queryWaysByName, {[39m
[31m+       name: args.roadName,[39m
[31m+       bounds: args.bbox,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     if (ways.length > 0) {[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         exists: true,[39m
[31m+         status: 'found' as const,[39m
[31m+         matches: ways.map((w: any) => ({[39m
[31m+           name: w.name || args.roadName,[39m
[31m+           highway: w.highwayClass || 'unknown',[39m
[31m+           surface: w.surface || null,[39m
[31m+           geometry: w.geometry.map((g: number[]) => ({ lat: g[1], lng: g[0] })),[39m
[31m+         })),[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   } catch (_error) {}[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Fall back to Overpass tool[39m
[31m+   return lookupRoad(args)[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ async function runCreateRouteSketch([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+   args: {[39m
[31m+     label: string[39m
[31m+     rationale: string[39m
[31m+     segments: {[39m
[31m+       roadName: string[39m
[31m+       fromName: string[39m
[31m+       toName: string[39m
[31m+       viaNames: string[] | null[39m
[31m+       fromLabel?: string[39m
[31m+       toLabel?: string[39m
[31m+     }[][39m
[31m+     anchorPoints: {[39m
[31m+       name: string[39m
[31m+       kind: 'town' | 'junction' | 'landmark' | 'pass'[39m
[31m+       lat: number[39m
[31m+       lng: number[39m
[31m+     }[][39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   // Store the sketch for use with compileSketch[39m
[31m+   const sessionId = ctx.planningSessionId[39m
[31m+   const sketch = {[39m
[31m+     label: args.label,[39m
[31m+     rationale: args.rationale,[39m
[31m+     segments: args.segments.map((s) => ({[39m
[31m+       roadName: s.roadName,[39m
[31m+       fromName: s.fromName,[39m
[31m+       toName: s.toName,[39m
[31m+       viaNames: s.viaNames || undefined,[39m
[31m+       fromLabel: s.fromLabel || undefined,[39m
[31m+       toLabel: s.toLabel || undefined,[39m
[31m+     })),[39m
[31m+     anchorPoints: args.anchorPoints,[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+   storePendingSketch(sessionId, sketch)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Return success so the agent knows the sketch was created[39m
[31m+   return {[39m
[31m+     type: 'sketch_created',[39m
[31m+     sketch,[39m
[31m+     message: `Route sketch "${args.label}" created. Now call compileSketch with start/end coordinates to generate the route.`,[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ async function runCompileSketch([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+   args: {[39m
[31m+     start: { lat: number; lng: number; label: string | null }[39m
[31m+     end: { lat: number; lng: number; label: string | null }[39m
[31m+     departureTime: number[39m
[31m+     preferences: {[39m
[31m+       scenicBias: 'default' | 'high'[39m
[31m+       avoidHighways: boolean[39m
[31m+       avoidTolls: boolean[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+     sketch?: {[39m
[31m+       label: string[39m
[31m+       rationale: string[39m
[31m+       segments: {[39m
[31m+         roadName: string[39m
[31m+         fromName: string[39m
[31m+         toName: string[39m
[31m+         viaNames?: string[][39m
[31m+         fromLabel?: string[39m
[31m+         toLabel?: string[39m
[31m+       }[][39m
[31m+       anchorPoints: {[39m
[31m+         name: string[39m
[31m+         kind: 'town' | 'junction' | 'landmark' | 'pass'[39m
[31m+         lat?: number[39m
[31m+         lng?: number[39m
[31m+       }[][39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   const sessionId = ctx.planningSessionId[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Get sketch from args or from pending store[39m
[31m+   let sketch = args.sketch[39m
[31m+   if (!sketch) {[39m
[31m+     sketch = getPendingSketch(sessionId)[39m
[31m+     if (!sketch) {[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         type: 'error',[39m
[31m+         message:[39m
[31m+           'No route sketch found. Call createRouteSketch first to define your route itinerary.',[39m
[31m+         hint: 'Use createRouteSketch to specify the roads and waypoints for your route.',[39m
[31m+         retryGuidance: 'create_sketch',[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Rate-limit check[39m
[31m+   const usage = await ctx.runQuery(internal.db.planUsage.checkUsageInternal, {[39m
[31m+     clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   if (!usage.allowed) {[39m
[31m+     return {[39m
[31m+       type: 'chat',[39m
[31m+       message: `You've reached your monthly limit of ${usage.limit} route plans. Upgrade to Premium for unlimited plans!`,[39m
[31m+       hint: 'Do not attempt another planRoute call — the user is rate-limited.',[39m
[31m+       retryGuidance: 'stop',[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Persist a route_plans row up front[39m
[31m+   const planInput = {[39m
[31m+     start: {[39m
[31m+       lat: args.start.lat,[39m
[31m+       lng: args.start.lng,[39m
[31m+       label: args.start.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+     },[39m
[31m+     end: {[39m
[31m+       lat: args.end.lat,[39m
[31m+       lng: args.end.lng,[39m
[31m+       label: args.end.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+     },[39m
[31m+     departureTime: args.departureTime,[39m
[31m+     preferences: args.preferences,[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   const { routePlanId } = await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.createForAgentInternal, {[39m
[31m+     clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+     planningSessionId: sessionId,[39m
[31m+     planInput,[39m
[31m+     startLabel: args.start.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+     endLabel: args.end.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Invalidate stale enrichments from previous route plans in this session[39m
[31m+   await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routeEnrichments.invalidateStaleEnrichments, {[39m
[31m+     planningSessionId: sessionId,[39m
[31m+     newRoutePlanId: routePlanId,[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   try {[39m
[31m+     let providerRoute: import('../providers/routingProvider').ProviderRouteResponse[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     if (sketch.segments.length > 0) {[39m
[31m+       // Per-segment compilation path (LLM-authored sketches)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // ------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+       // Retry tracking (US-025)[39m
[31m+       // ------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+       // Load current session state (attempt count + previously-succeeded segments)[39m
[31m+       const currentState = getPendingSketchState(sessionId)[39m
[31m+       const attemptCount = (currentState?.attemptCount ?? 0) + 1[39m
[31m+       const cachedSucceeded: CachedSegmentResult[] = currentState?.succeededSegments ?? [][39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Determine which segments need compilation this attempt.[39m
[31m+       // Unchanged segments (same roadName+fromName+toName as a cached success) are skipped.[39m
[31m+       const newSegments: SegmentIdentity[] = sketch.segments.map((s: any) => ({[39m
[31m+         roadName: s.roadName,[39m
[31m+         fromName: s.fromName,[39m
[31m+         toName: s.toName,[39m
[31m+       }))[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       const unchanged = findUnchangedSegments(newSegments, cachedSucceeded)[39m
[31m+       const toCompile = sketch.segments.filter((_: any, i: number) => !unchanged.has(i))[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // ------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+       // Max retries exhausted with persistent failures[39m
[31m+       // ------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+       const attemptsRemaining = MAX_COMPILE_ATTEMPTS - attemptCount[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       if ([39m
[31m+         attemptCount >= MAX_COMPILE_ATTEMPTS &&[39m
[31m+         cachedSucceeded.length > 0 &&[39m
[31m+         toCompile.length > 0[39m
[31m+       ) {[39m
[31m+         // Compile the remaining failed segments one last time to see if any succeed[39m
[31m+         const lastResults = await compileSegments({[39m
[31m+           planInput,[39m
[31m+           sketch: { ...sketch, segments: toCompile },[39m
[31m+           locationBias: ctx.currentLocation,[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+         const allResults = mergeSegmentResults(newSegments, unchanged, lastResults)[39m
[31m+         const stillFailed = allResults.filter((r) => r.status === 'failed')[39m
[31m+         const nowSucceeded = allResults.filter((r) => r.status === 'ok')[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         if (stillFailed.length > 0 && nowSucceeded.length > 0) {[39m
[31m+           // Build a partial route from the succeeded segments and return it with a message[39m
[31m+           const partialRoute = stitchSegments(nowSucceeded)[39m
[31m+           const routeSnapshot = await normalizeRoute({[39m
[31m+             providerRoute: partialRoute,[39m
[31m+             planInput,[39m
[31m+             sketch,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+           const results = [{ routeSnapshot, sketch }][39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           let built[39m
[31m+           try {[39m
[31m+             built = buildOptionsFromResults(results, crypto.randomUUID())[39m
[31m+           } catch (buildError) {[39m
[31m+             await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+               routePlanId,[39m
[31m+               status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+               errorMessage: `Failed to build route options: ${buildError instanceof Error ? buildError.message : String(buildError)}`,[39m
[31m+             })[39m
[31m+             throw buildError[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           clearPendingSketch(sessionId)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           try {[39m
[31m+             await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+               routePlanId,[39m
[31m+               status: 'completed',[39m
[31m+               result: built,[39m
[31m+             })[39m
[31m+           } catch (updateError) {[39m
[31m+             throw updateError[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.planUsage.incrementUsageInternal, {[39m
[31m+             clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           const failedRoadNames = stillFailed[39m
[31m+             .map((f) => newSegments[f.segmentIndex]?.roadName ?? 'unknown road')[39m
[31m+             .join(', ')[39m
[31m+           return {[39m
[31m+             type: 'routes',[39m
[31m+             data: {[39m
[31m+               ...built,[39m
[31m+               message: `I routed most of the trip but couldn't find a path for ${failedRoadNames}. Here's what works.`,[39m
[31m+             },[39m
[31m+             routePlanId,[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         if (stillFailed.length > 0 && nowSucceeded.length === 0) {[39m
[31m+           // All remaining segments failed — return a chat message[39m
[31m+           clearPendingSketch(sessionId)[39m
[31m+           await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+             routePlanId,[39m
[31m+             status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+             errorMessage: `All segments failed after ${MAX_COMPILE_ATTEMPTS} attempts`,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+           const failedRoadNames = stillFailed[39m
[31m+             .map((f) => newSegments[f.segmentIndex]?.roadName ?? 'unknown road')[39m
[31m+             .join(', ')[39m
[31m+           return {[39m
[31m+             type: 'chat',[39m
[31m+             message: `I wasn't able to find a path for ${failedRoadNames} after several attempts. Try a different route?`,[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         // All succeeded on last attempt — fall through to normal success path[39m
[31m+         providerRoute = stitchSegments(nowSucceeded)[39m
[31m+         clearPendingSketch(sessionId)[39m
[31m+         const routeSnapshot = await normalizeRoute({ providerRoute, planInput, sketch })[39m
[31m+         const results = [{ routeSnapshot, sketch }][39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         let built[39m
[31m+         try {[39m
[31m+           built = buildOptionsFromResults(results, crypto.randomUUID())[39m
[31m+         } catch (buildError) {[39m
[31m+           await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+             routePlanId,[39m
[31m+             status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+             errorMessage: `Failed to build route options: ${buildError instanceof Error ? buildError.message : String(buildError)}`,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+           throw buildError[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         try {[39m
[31m+           await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+             routePlanId,[39m
[31m+             status: 'completed',[39m
[31m+             result: built,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+         } catch (updateError) {[39m
[31m+           throw updateError[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.planUsage.incrementUsageInternal, {[39m
[31m+           clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+         await persistRoutingCard(ctx, routePlanId)[39m
[31m+         return { type: 'routes', data: built, routePlanId }[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // ------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+       // Normal compilation attempt (attempt 1..MAX-1, or first attempt with no cache)[39m
[31m+       // ------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+       const segmentResults = await compileSegments({[39m
[31m+         planInput,[39m
[31m+         sketch: { ...sketch, segments: toCompile },[39m
[31m+         locationBias: ctx.currentLocation,[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Merge new results with cached unchanged segments[39m
[31m+       const mergedResults = mergeSegmentResults(newSegments, unchanged, segmentResults)[39m
[31m+       const failed = mergedResults.filter((r) => r.status === 'failed')[39m
[31m+       const succeeded = mergedResults.filter((r) => r.status === 'ok')[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       if (failed.length > 0) {[39m
[31m+         // Total failure: all segments failed - throw exception to terminate agent[39m
[31m+         if (succeeded.length === 0) {[39m
[31m+           const errorDetails = failed.map((f) => ({[39m
[31m+             segmentIndex: f.segmentIndex,[39m
[31m+             roadName: newSegments[f.segmentIndex].roadName,[39m
[31m+             fromName: newSegments[f.segmentIndex].fromName,[39m
[31m+             toName: newSegments[f.segmentIndex].toName,[39m
[31m+             error: f.status === 'failed' ? f.error : 'unknown',[39m
[31m+           }))[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+             routePlanId,[39m
[31m+             status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+             errorMessage: `All ${failed.length} segments failed to route`,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+           throw new Error([39m
[31m+             `All road segments couldn't be routed. ` +[39m
[31m+               `Failed segments: ${errorDetails.map((e) => `${e.roadName} (${e.fromName} → ${e.toName}): ${e.error}`).join(', ')}. ` +[39m
[31m+               `Try using more specific location names or major highways.`,[39m
[31m+           )[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         // Partial failure: some segments succeeded - return error for retry[39m
[31m+         // Update the succeeded segment cache for the next retry attempt[39m
[31m+         const newCachedSucceeded: CachedSegmentResult[] = succeeded.map((s) => ({[39m
[31m+           segmentIndex: s.segmentIndex,[39m
[31m+           route: (s as Extract<typeof s, { status: 'ok' }>).route,[39m
[31m+           identity: newSegments[s.segmentIndex],[39m
[31m+         }))[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         updatePendingSketchState(sessionId, {[39m
[31m+           sketch,[39m
[31m+           succeededSegments: newCachedSucceeded,[39m
[31m+           attemptCount,[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+           status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+           errorMessage: `${failed.length} of ${newSegments.length} segments failed`,[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         return {[39m
[31m+           type: 'error',[39m
[31m+           message: `${failed.length} of ${newSegments.length} road segments couldn't be routed.`,[39m
[31m+           hint: JSON.stringify({[39m
[31m+             type: 'partial_route',[39m
[31m+             attemptsRemaining,[39m
[31m+             succeeded: succeeded.map((s) => ({[39m
[31m+               segmentIndex: s.segmentIndex,[39m
[31m+               roadName: newSegments[s.segmentIndex].roadName,[39m
[31m+             })),[39m
[31m+             failed: failed.map((f) => ({[39m
[31m+               segmentIndex: f.segmentIndex,[39m
[31m+               roadName: newSegments[f.segmentIndex].roadName,[39m
[31m+               fromName: newSegments[f.segmentIndex].fromName,[39m
[31m+               toName: newSegments[f.segmentIndex].toName,[39m
[31m+               error: f.status === 'failed' ? f.error : 'unknown',[39m
[31m+             })),[39m
[31m+             retryGuidance: 'revise_failed_segments',[39m
[31m+             hint: 'Revise only the failed segments. Keep succeeded segments unchanged.',[39m
[31m+           }),[39m
[31m+           retryGuidance: 'revise_failed_segments',[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // All segments succeeded — stitch into a single provider route[39m
[31m+       providerRoute = stitchSegments(mergedResults)[39m
[31m+     } else {[39m
[31m+       // Single-shot compilation path (deterministic orchestrator sketches with empty segments)[39m
[31m+       providerRoute = await compileSketchImpl({[39m
[31m+         planInput,[39m
[31m+         sketch,[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Normalize the route[39m
[31m+     const routeSnapshot = await normalizeRoute({[39m
[31m+       providerRoute,[39m
[31m+       planInput,[39m
[31m+       sketch,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Build the result[39m
[31m+     const results = [[39m
[31m+       {[39m
[31m+         routeSnapshot,[39m
[31m+         sketch,[39m
[31m+       },[39m
[31m+     ][39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     let built[39m
[31m+     try {[39m
[31m+       built = buildOptionsFromResults(results, crypto.randomUUID())[39m
[31m+     } catch (buildError) {[39m
[31m+       await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+         routePlanId,[39m
[31m+         status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+         errorMessage: `Failed to build route options: ${buildError instanceof Error ? buildError.message : String(buildError)}`,[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+       throw buildError[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Clear the pending sketch after successful compilation[39m
[31m+     clearPendingSketch(sessionId)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Finalize the route_plans row[39m
[31m+     try {[39m
[31m+       await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+         routePlanId,[39m
[31m+         status: 'completed',[39m
[31m+         result: built,[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+     } catch (updateError) {[39m
[31m+       throw updateError[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Increment usage[39m
[31m+     await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.planUsage.incrementUsageInternal, {[39m
[31m+       clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     await persistRoutingCard(ctx, routePlanId)[39m
[31m+     return { type: 'routes', data: built, routePlanId }[39m
[31m+   } catch (error) {[39m
[31m+     const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Check if it's a routing compilation error (e.g., invalid road, no connection)[39m
[31m+     const isRoutingError =[39m
[31m+       errorMessage.includes('ROUTING_COMPILE_FAILED') ||[39m
[31m+       errorMessage.includes('ZERO_RESULTS') ||[39m
[31m+       errorMessage.includes('NOT_FOUND')[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+       routePlanId,[39m
[31m+       status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+       errorMessage,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     if (isRoutingError) {[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         type: 'error',[39m
[31m+         message:[39m
[31m+           "I couldn't route that way — the roads may not connect or one might not exist. Let me try a different approach.",[39m
[31m+         hint: `The route sketch "${sketch.label}" couldn't be compiled. Try using different roads or check if they connect.`,[39m
[31m+         retryGuidance: 'revise_sketch',[39m
[31m+         routePlanId,[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     return {[39m
[31m+       type: 'error',[39m
[31m+       message: "I couldn't plan your route right now. Please try again.",[39m
[31m+       hint:[39m
[31m+         error instanceof Error && error.message.includes('timeout')[39m
[31m+           ? 'The route calculation timed out. Try a shorter distance or simpler route.'[39m
[31m+           : 'Suggest an alternate destination or relax preferences (e.g. remove avoid-highways).',[39m
[31m+       retryGuidance: 'ask_rider',[39m
[31m+       routePlanId,[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ async function runPlanRoute([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+   args: {[39m
[31m+     start: { lat: number; lng: number; label: string | null }[39m
[31m+     end: { lat: number; lng: number; label: string | null }[39m
[31m+     departureTime: number[39m
[31m+     preferences: {[39m
[31m+       scenicBias: 'default' | 'high'[39m
[31m+       avoidHighways: boolean[39m
[31m+       avoidTolls: boolean[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+   executeCtx?: ExecuteContext,[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   // Rate-limit check (limit configurable via RATE_LIMIT_OVERRIDE env var; 0 = unlimited)[39m
[31m+   const usage = await ctx.runQuery(internal.db.planUsage.checkUsageInternal, {[39m
[31m+     clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   if (!usage.allowed) {[39m
[31m+     return {[39m
[31m+       type: 'chat',[39m
[31m+       message: `You've reached your monthly limit of ${usage.limit} route plans. Upgrade to Premium for unlimited plans!`,[39m
[31m+       hint: 'Do not attempt another planRoute call — the user is rate-limited.',[39m
[31m+       retryGuidance: 'stop',[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Persist a route_plans row up front so the reactive RoutingCard in the[39m
[31m+   // chat transcript can subscribe to status/phase/result updates.[39m
[31m+   const planInput = {[39m
[31m+     start: {[39m
[31m+       lat: args.start.lat,[39m
[31m+       lng: args.start.lng,[39m
[31m+       label: args.start.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+     },[39m
[31m+     end: {[39m
[31m+       lat: args.end.lat,[39m
[31m+       lng: args.end.lng,[39m
[31m+       label: args.end.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+     },[39m
[31m+     departureTime: args.departureTime,[39m
[31m+     preferences: args.preferences,[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   const { routePlanId } = await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.createForAgentInternal, {[39m
[31m+     clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+     planningSessionId: ctx.planningSessionId,[39m
[31m+     planInput,[39m
[31m+     startLabel: args.start.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+     endLabel: args.end.label ?? undefined,[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Invalidate stale enrichments from previous route plans in this session[39m
[31m+   await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routeEnrichments.invalidateStaleEnrichments, {[39m
[31m+     planningSessionId: ctx.planningSessionId,[39m
[31m+     newRoutePlanId: routePlanId,[39m
[31m+   })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Retry orchestrator internally before surfacing errors to the agent/UI.[39m
[31m+   // This prevents the UI from flashing a failure while the agent retries[39m
[31m+   // with a brand-new plan record.[39m
[31m+   const MAX_ORCHESTRATOR_RETRIES = 2[39m
[31m+   let _lastError: unknown = null[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   for (let attempt = 1; attempt <= MAX_ORCHESTRATOR_RETRIES; attempt++) {[39m
[31m+     try {[39m
[31m+       const results = await planRideOrchestrator({[39m
[31m+         planInput,[39m
[31m+         departureTimeMs: args.departureTime,[39m
[31m+         onProgress: async (event: PlanRideProgressEvent) => {[39m
[31m+           if (event.type === 'start') {[39m
[31m+             await executeCtx?.onSubToolPending?.(event.toolName, 'routing')[39m
[31m+             return[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+           await executeCtx?.onSubToolComplete?.([39m
[31m+             event.toolName,[39m
[31m+             'routing',[39m
[31m+             event.summary,[39m
[31m+             event.durationMs,[39m
[31m+           )[39m
[31m+         },[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       let built[39m
[31m+       try {[39m
[31m+         built = buildOptionsFromResults(results, crypto.randomUUID())[39m
[31m+       } catch (buildError) {[39m
[31m+         await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+           status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+           errorMessage: `Failed to build route options: ${buildError instanceof Error ? buildError.message : String(buildError)}`,[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+         // Build errors are not retryable — bad data, not transient[39m
[31m+         return {[39m
[31m+           type: 'error',[39m
[31m+           message: "I couldn't plan your route right now. Please try again.",[39m
[31m+           hint: 'There was an issue processing the route data.',[39m
[31m+           retryGuidance: 'ask_rider',[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       try {[39m
[31m+         // Check if the route plan was already cancelled or failed (e.g., agent returned needs_clarification)[39m
[31m+         const currentPlan = (await ctx.runQuery(internal.db.routePlans.getPlanByIdInternal, {[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+         })) as any[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+         // Only update to completed if not already cancelled or failed[39m
[31m+         if (currentPlan?.status !== 'cancelled' && currentPlan?.status !== 'failed') {[39m
[31m+           await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+             routePlanId,[39m
[31m+             status: 'completed',[39m
[31m+             result: built,[39m
[31m+           })[39m
[31m+         } else {[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+       } catch (updateError) {[39m
[31m+         throw updateError[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Increment usage (deterministic action)[39m
[31m+       await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.planUsage.incrementUsageInternal, {[39m
[31m+         clerkUserId: ctx.clerkUserId,[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       await persistRoutingCard(ctx, routePlanId)[39m
[31m+       return { type: 'routes', data: built, routePlanId }[39m
[31m+     } catch (error) {[39m
[31m+       _lastError = error[39m
[31m+       const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       if (attempt < MAX_ORCHESTRATOR_RETRIES) {[39m
[31m+         // Update status to show retry in progress (not "failed")[39m
[31m+         await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+           status: 'running',[39m
[31m+           statusMessage: 'Retrying route planning...',[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+         continue[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Check if the route plan was already completed or cancelled (race condition guard)[39m
[31m+       const currentPlan = (await ctx.runQuery(internal.db.routePlans.getPlanByIdInternal, {[39m
[31m+         routePlanId,[39m
[31m+       })) as any[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Only mark as failed if not already completed or cancelled[39m
[31m+       if (currentPlan?.status !== 'completed' && currentPlan?.status !== 'cancelled') {[39m
[31m+         await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+           routePlanId,[39m
[31m+           status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+           errorMessage,[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+       } else {[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         type: 'error',[39m
[31m+         message: "I couldn't plan your route right now. Please try again.",[39m
[31m+         hint:[39m
[31m+           error instanceof Error && error.message.includes('timeout')[39m
[31m+             ? 'The route calculation timed out. Try a shorter distance or simpler route.'[39m
[31m+             : 'Suggest an alternate destination or relax preferences (e.g. remove avoid-highways).',[39m
[31m+         retryGuidance: 'ask_rider',[39m
[31m+         routePlanId,[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Should never reach here, but TypeScript needs it[39m
[31m+   return {[39m
[31m+     type: 'error',[39m
[31m+     message: "I couldn't plan your route right now. Please try again.",[39m
[31m+     hint: 'Suggest an alternate destination or relax preferences.',[39m
[31m+     retryGuidance: 'ask_rider',[39m
[31m+     routePlanId,[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Set the title of the current planning session.[39m
[31m+  * Called by the agent after creating a route to give the session a meaningful name.[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ async function runSetSessionTitle(ctx: AgentContext, args: { title: string }): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   try {[39m
[31m+     await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.planningSessions.updateSessionTitle, {[39m
[31m+       sessionId: ctx.planningSessionId,[39m
[31m+       title: args.title,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     return { type: 'confirmation', message: 'Session title updated' }[39m
[31m+   } catch (error) {[39m
[31m+     return {[39m
[31m+       type: 'error',[39m
[31m+       message: "I couldn't update the session title.",[39m
[31m+       hint: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // Tool Definitions[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ type RoutingTool = Tool & { parallelSafe: boolean }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ const routingTools: RoutingTool[] = [[39m
[31m+   {[39m
[31m+     name: 'geocode',[39m
[31m+     description:[39m
[31m+       'Look up coordinates for a place name, address, or landmark. Use before planRoute or compileSketch when the rider names somewhere other than "here". Results are biased toward the rider\'s current location.',[39m
[31m+     parameters: AgentToolSchemas.geocode as any,[39m
[31m+     parallelSafe: true,[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+   {[39m
[31m+     name: 'createRouteSketch',[39m
[31m+     description:[39m
[31m+       'Create a high-level route itinerary by specifying road segments (think "take Highway 5 to Highway 405 to PCH"). Use this when the rider asks to avoid specific roads ("avoid Highway 1") or requests a particular route ("take Skyline Blvd"). After creating the sketch, call compileSketch with start/end coordinates to generate the precise route.',[39m
[31m+     parameters: AgentToolSchemas.createRouteSketch as any,[39m
[31m+     parallelSafe: true,[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+   {[39m
[31m+     name: 'compileSketch',[39m
[31m+     description:[39m
[31m+       'Convert a route sketch into a precise route with geometry from Google Maps. Call geocode first if you need coordinates for start/end points. This validates that your sketch roads actually connect and returns detailed turn-by-turn geometry. If routing fails, revise your sketch and try again.',[39m
[31m+     parameters: AgentToolSchemas.compileSketch as any,[39m
[31m+     parallelSafe: false,[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+   {[39m
[31m+     name: 'planRoute',[39m
[31m+     description:[39m
[31m+       'Plan a motorcycle route with 2-3 scenic options using the deterministic orchestrator. Call geocode first if you need coordinates for the start or end. Use the rider\'s current location (given in the system prompt) as start when they say "here" or don\'t specify. For refinements, consider using createRouteSketch + compileSketch for more control.',[39m
[31m+     parameters: AgentToolSchemas.planRoute as any,[39m
[31m+     parallelSafe: false,[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+   {[39m
[31m+     name: 'setSessionTitle',[39m
[31m+     description:[39m
[31m+       "Set the title of the current planning session based on the route context. Use this after creating a route to give the session a meaningful name (e.g., 'SF to Oakland Ride', 'Scenic Coast Route'). The title should reflect the route's origin, destination, or character.",[39m
[31m+     parameters: {[39m
[31m+       type: 'object',[39m
[31m+       properties: {[39m
[31m+         title: {[39m
[31m+           type: 'string',[39m
[31m+           description:[39m
[31m+             'The session title (e.g., "SF to Oakland Ride", "Scenic Coast Route", "Morning Commute")',[39m
[31m+         },[39m
[31m+       },[39m
[31m+       required: ['title'],[39m
[31m+     } as any,[39m
[31m+     parallelSafe: true,[39m
[31m+   },[39m
[31m+ ][39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ const routingParallelSafeTools = new Set([39m
[31m+   routingTools.filter((t) => t.parallelSafe).map((t) => t.name),[39m
[31m+ )[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // Tool Dispatcher[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export async function executeRoutingTool([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+   call: ToolCall,[39m
[31m+   executeCtx?: ExecuteContext,[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<unknown> {[39m
[31m+   const validated = validateToolCall(routingTools, call)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Notify caller that tool is starting; capture any pending card messageId[39m
[31m+   let pendingMessageId: Id<'session_messages'> | undefined[39m
[31m+   if (executeCtx?.onToolStart) {[39m
[31m+     const startResult = await executeCtx.onToolStart(call.name, validated)[39m
[31m+     if (startResult) {[39m
[31m+       pendingMessageId = startResult.messageId[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   let result: unknown[39m
[31m+   try {[39m
[31m+     switch (call.name) {[39m
[31m+       case 'geocode':[39m
[31m+         result = await runGeocode(ctx, validated)[39m
[31m+         break[39m
[31m+       case 'createRouteSketch':[39m
[31m+         result = await runCreateRouteSketch(ctx, validated)[39m
[31m+         break[39m
[31m+       case 'compileSketch':[39m
[31m+         result = await runCompileSketch(ctx, validated)[39m
[31m+         break[39m
[31m+       case 'planRoute':[39m
[31m+         result = await runPlanRoute(ctx, validated, executeCtx)[39m
[31m+         break[39m
[31m+       case 'setSessionTitle':[39m
[31m+         result = await runSetSessionTitle(ctx, validated)[39m
[31m+         break[39m
[31m+       default:[39m
[31m+         result = { type: 'error', message: `Unknown tool: ${call.name}` }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   } catch (err) {[39m
[31m+     // Re-throw after notifying so the agent loop's error handler still fires[39m
[31m+     if (executeCtx?.onToolFinish) {[39m
[31m+       await executeCtx.onToolFinish(call.id, call.name, pendingMessageId, {[39m
[31m+         type: 'error',[39m
[31m+         message: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),[39m
[31m+         hint: "An unexpected error occurred. Ask the rider what they'd like to do.",[39m
[31m+         retryGuidance: 'ask_rider',[39m
[31m+       })[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+     throw err[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   if (executeCtx?.onToolFinish) {[39m
[31m+     await executeCtx.onToolFinish(call.id, call.name, pendingMessageId, result)[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   return result[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // Start Location Context[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export type DefaultStartContext = {[39m
[31m+   lat: number[39m
[31m+   lng: number[39m
[31m+   label: string[39m
[31m+   source: 'current' | 'lastKnown'[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * The rider's default origin context: live currentLocation if present, otherwise the[39m
[31m+  * session's lastKnownLocation (possibly stale). This is context for the agent, not[39m
[31m+  * intent parsing. The agent still decides whether the rider named an explicit origin.[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export async function getDefaultStartContext([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<DefaultStartContext | null> {[39m
[31m+   if (ctx.currentLocation) {[39m
[31m+     return { ...ctx.currentLocation, label: 'Current Location', source: 'current' }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+   try {[39m
[31m+     const sessionData = await ctx.runQuery(api.db.planningSessions.getSessionById, {[39m
[31m+       sessionId: ctx.planningSessionId,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+     const lk = sessionData?.lastKnownLocation[39m
[31m+     if (lk) return { lat: lk.lat, lng: lk.lng, label: 'Last Known Location', source: 'lastKnown' }[39m
[31m+   } catch {[39m
[31m+     // Silently ignore lookup failures — fall through to "no location".[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+   return null[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ export function isStartLocationClarification(question: string): boolean {[39m
[31m+   const normalized = question.toLowerCase()[39m
[31m+   return ([39m
[31m+     /\bwhere\b.{0,40}\b(start|starting|begin|beginning|leav|depart|origin)\b/.test(normalized) ||[39m
[31m+     /\b(start|starting|origin)\b.{0,40}\b(where|from|location|point)\b/.test(normalized) ||[39m
[31m+     /\bwhich\s+(part|area|neighborhood|neighbourhood)\b.{0,40}\b(start|starting|from)\b/.test([39m
[31m+       normalized,[39m
[31m+     )[39m
[31m+   )[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // Routing Prompt[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Build the routing sub-agent system prompt.[39m
[31m+  * Phase 1 only — no enrichment instructions.[39m
[31m+  *[39m
[31m+  * Async to support lastKnownLocation lookup when currentLocation is undefined.[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export async function buildRoutingPrompt([39m
[31m+   ctx: AgentContext,[39m
[31m+   defaultStartContext?: DefaultStartContext | null,[39m
[31m+ ): Promise<string> {[39m
[31m+   let locBlock: string[39m
[31m+   const startContext =[39m
[31m+     defaultStartContext === undefined ? await getDefaultStartContext(ctx) : defaultStartContext[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   if (startContext) {[39m
[31m+     const freshness =[39m
[31m+       startContext.source === 'lastKnown'[39m
[31m+         ? 'This may be stale, so prefer a clearly named origin if the rider gives one.'[39m
[31m+         : 'This is live device context.'[39m
[31m+     locBlock = `The rider has default origin context: lat=${startContext.lat}, lng=${startContext.lng} (label: "${startContext.label}"). ${freshness}[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ You are responsible for natural-language intent. Do NOT rely on string-shape rules. Use the rider's words, location, and conversation context to decide whether they named an explicit origin or only a destination.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ Origin policy:[39m
[31m+ - If the rider gives only a destination or an ambiguous route idea, use the default origin above. NEVER ask "where are you starting from?" when this default origin is available.[39m
[31m+ - If the rider appears to name an origin and destination, geocode BOTH named places and use those results. Example: near the Bay Area, "SF to Santacruze" means San Francisco, CA to Santa Cruz, CA.[39m
[31m+ - If context makes a phrase look like a place/business lookup rather than a route, do not force route semantics; ask a concise clarification.[39m
[31m+ - Normalize common place shorthand when you geocode: SF/S.F. = San Francisco, CA; DFW = Dallas-Fort Worth, TX; NY/NYC = New York City, NY; Santacruze = Santa Cruz, CA.[39m
[31m+ - Use context first, clarify only when the route cannot be planned from the available context.`[39m
[31m+   } else {[39m
[31m+     locBlock = `Rider's current location: unknown. If the rider gives an explicit origin and destination, that is a COMPLETE route request: "SF to Santacruze", "from DFW to Austin", and "NY to Bear Mountain" all go straight to routing.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ You are responsible for natural-language intent. Normalize common place shorthand when you geocode: SF/S.F. = San Francisco, CA; DFW = Dallas-Fort Worth, TX; NY/NYC = New York City, NY; Santacruze = Santa Cruz, CA. Ask where they are starting from only for destination-only route requests that do not name an origin.`[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   return Promise.resolve(`You are an expert motorcycle navigator with strong opinions about the best routes — think of yourself as a local who has ridden every road in the area. Be concise — 1-2 sentences per response. Use 2nd person ("your ride", "you'll see").[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ${locBlock}[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ## Your Job: Plan Routes Fast[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ Your primary tool is planRoute — it generates 2-3 scenic route options using AI-suggested roads. Use it for most requests.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **When to use planRoute** (95% of requests):[39m
[31m+ - "scenic ride to Santa Cruz"[39m
[31m+ - "take me somewhere fun"[39m
[31m+ - "2-hour ride from here"[39m
[31m+ - Any destination request[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **When to use createRouteSketch + compileSketch** (advanced control):[39m
[31m+ - Rider specifies exact roads: "take Highway 1 to PCH"[39m
[31m+ - Rider wants to avoid a specific road: "avoid I-5"[39m
[31m+ - Rider requests a particular route style you can't achieve with planRoute[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **Workflow for sketching** (only when rider specifies roads):[39m
[31m+ 1. If the rider names a place (not "here"), call geocode first to get coordinates.[39m
[31m+ 2. Call createRouteSketch with specific road names and anchor points.[39m
[31m+ 3. Call compileSketch with start/end coordinates to generate the route.[39m
[31m+ 4. Present in 1-2 sentences.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **CRITICAL: Always pass location labels**:[39m
[31m+ - When calling planRoute or compileSketch after geocoding, ALWAYS include the label from geocode results[39m
[31m+ - Example: planRoute({ start: {..., label: "San Francisco, CA"}, end: {..., label: "Santa Cruz, CA"}, ... })[39m
[31m+ - This ensures route cards show meaningful location names instead of coordinates[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **How to author a sketch**:[39m
[31m+ - Fill in segments with specific road names: roadName, fromName, toName[39m
[31m+ - Add fromLabel/toLabel for more descriptive presentation labels (e.g., "Downtown San Jose" instead of just "San Jose")[39m
[31m+ - Use viaNames to include intermediate landmarks — e.g., "Skeggs Point" on Skyline Blvd[39m
[31m+ - Add anchorPoints for key junctions, towns, passes, or landmarks[39m
[31m+ - Each anchorPoint kind MUST be: "town", "junction", "landmark", or "pass"[39m
[31m+ - ALL anchor points MUST have lat/lng from geocode results[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **Segment retry (CRITICAL)**: When compileSketch returns a partial_route error:[39m
[31m+ - Call compileSketch AGAIN with a revised sketch that keeps succeeded segments IDENTICAL[39m
[31m+ - Only change failed segments — try different endpoints or add viaNames[39m
[31m+ - Do NOT call createRouteSketch to start over — compileSketch caches succeeded segments[39m
[31m+ - If the same segment fails 3 times, fall back to planRoute for that leg[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **IMPORTANT: If a tool call fails with a validation error, fix the arguments and retry. Do NOT give up after one failure.**[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **Examples**:[39m
[31m+ - "Scenic ride to Santa Cruz" → geocode("Santa Cruz") → planRoute(start: {..., label: "Current Location"}, end: {..., label: "Santa Cruz, CA"}) → done[39m
[31m+ - "Take Highway 1 south" → geocode → createRouteSketch with Highway 1 → compileSketch(start: {..., label: "..."}, end: {..., label: "..."}) → done[39m
[31m+ - "Avoid the freeway, get to Napa" → geocode → createRouteSketch with backroads → compileSketch(start: {..., label: "..."}, end: {..., label: "Napa, CA"}) → done[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **Presentation**:[39m
[31m+ - 1-2 sentences, highlight scenic features, road types, rough duration.[39m
[31m+ - Never expose tool names or technical details to the rider.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **Session Naming**:[39m
[31m+ - After creating a route with planRoute, call setSessionTitle to give the session a meaningful name[39m
[31m+ - Use format: "{Origin} to {Destination} Ride" (e.g., "SF to Oakland Ride")[39m
[31m+ - Or use route character: "Scenic Coast Route", "Mountain Loop", etc.[39m
[31m+ - This helps riders identify their sessions in the session list[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ **Errors**: suggest what the rider can try next without surfacing internals.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ When done, respond with a JSON summary:[39m
[31m+ {"status": "route_ready", "routePlanId": "<id>", "summary": "<1-2 sentence summary>"}[39m
[31m+ OR if clarification needed:[39m
[31m+ {"status": "needs_clarification", "question": "<what you need to know>"}[39m
[31m+ OR if failed:[39m
[31m+ {"status": "failed", "reason": "<why it failed>"}`)[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+ // Main Entry Point[39m
[31m+ // -----------------------------------------------------------------------------[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ /**[39m
[31m+  * Execute the routing sub-agent.[39m
[31m+  * Owns route creation: geocoding, sketch authoring, compilation, and planRoute fallback.[39m
[31m+  */[39m
[31m+ export async function executeRoutingAgent(config: SubAgentConfig): Promise<RoutingAgentResult> {[39m
[31m+   const { ctx, executeCtx, budgetTracker, userMessage } = config[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Routing agent uses low-reasoning model for latency — narrower tool set and focused prompt compensate[39m
[31m+   const model = getAgentModel('low')[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Deterministic code supplies context only. The routing agent owns intent parsing:[39m
[31m+   // whether "SF" is an origin, destination, business name, or needs clarification.[39m
[31m+   const defaultStartContext = await getDefaultStartContext(ctx)[39m
[31m+   const systemPrompt = await buildRoutingPrompt(ctx, defaultStartContext)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // One routing attempt: run the sub-agent on `attemptMessage` and interpret its output.[39m
[31m+   const attempt = async (attemptMessage: string): Promise<RoutingAgentResult> => {[39m
[31m+     const context = {[39m
[31m+       systemPrompt,[39m
[31m+       // Sub-agent gets NO conversation history — only the current user message[39m
[31m+       messages: [{ role: 'user' as const, content: attemptMessage, timestamp: Date.now() }],[39m
[31m+       tools: routingTools,[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     const result = await runAgent({[39m
[31m+       model,[39m
[31m+       context,[39m
[31m+       executor: (call: ToolCall) => executeRoutingTool(ctx, call, executeCtx),[39m
[31m+       callbacks: executeCtx[39m
[31m+         ? {[39m
[31m+             onToolStart: executeCtx.onToolStart,[39m
[31m+             onToolFinish: executeCtx.onToolFinish,[39m
[31m+             onAgentTurn: executeCtx.onAgentTurn,[39m
[31m+             onToolResultPiMessage: executeCtx.onToolResultPiMessage,[39m
[31m+             // NOT forwarding onTextDelta or onThinkingDelta — sub-agent text doesn't stream to UI[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+         : undefined,[39m
[31m+       maxSteps: 20, // uncapped for now — levelsetting resource needs[39m
[31m+       timeoutMs: 300_000, // 5 min — uncapped for levelsetting[39m
[31m+       budgetTracker,[39m
[31m+       parallelSafeTools: routingParallelSafeTools,[39m
[31m+     })[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Determine result from tool results and response text[39m
[31m+     const attachments = extractRouteAttachments(result.toolResults)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     if (attachments.length > 0 && attachments[0].routePlanId) {[39m
[31m+       const summary = result.response || 'Route ready!'[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         status: 'route_ready',[39m
[31m+         routePlanId: attachments[0].routePlanId,[39m
[31m+         summary,[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     if (result.response && result.toolResults.length === 0) {[39m
[31m+       // Agent responded with text but no tool calls — treat as a clarification request.[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         status: 'needs_clarification',[39m
[31m+         question: result.response,[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // Try to parse structured result from response text[39m
[31m+     if (result.response) {[39m
[31m+       try {[39m
[31m+         const parsed = JSON.parse(result.response)[39m
[31m+         if (parsed.status === 'route_ready' && parsed.routePlanId) {[39m
[31m+           return {[39m
[31m+             status: 'route_ready',[39m
[31m+             routePlanId: parsed.routePlanId,[39m
[31m+             summary: parsed.summary ?? '',[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+         if (parsed.status === 'needs_clarification' && parsed.question) {[39m
[31m+           // Agent explicitly returned needs_clarification as JSON[39m
[31m+           // If any route plans were created in tool results, mark them as cancelled[39m
[31m+           // since the agent interrupted the plan to ask for more info[39m
[31m+           for (const tr of result.toolResults) {[39m
[31m+             const toolResult = tr.result as any[39m
[31m+             if (toolResult?.routePlanId) {[39m
[31m+               await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+                 routePlanId: toolResult.routePlanId,[39m
[31m+                 status: 'cancelled',[39m
[31m+                 errorMessage: parsed.question ?? 'Agent needs clarification',[39m
[31m+               })[39m
[31m+               break[39m
[31m+             }[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+           return { status: 'needs_clarification', question: parsed.question }[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+         if (parsed.status === 'failed') {[39m
[31m+           // Update any route plan that was created before the failure[39m
[31m+           for (const tr of result.toolResults) {[39m
[31m+             const toolResult = tr.result as any[39m
[31m+             if (toolResult?.routePlanId) {[39m
[31m+               await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+                 routePlanId: toolResult.routePlanId,[39m
[31m+                 status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+                 errorMessage: parsed.reason ?? 'Unknown failure',[39m
[31m+               })[39m
[31m+               break[39m
[31m+             }[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+           return { status: 'failed', reason: parsed.reason ?? 'Unknown failure' }[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+       } catch {[39m
[31m+         // Not JSON — fall through to handle unstructured response[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Agent responded with non-JSON text but has tool results[39m
[31m+       // This is an error - the agent should return structured JSON when it calls tools[39m
[31m+       if (result.toolResults.length > 0) {[39m
[31m+         // Mark any created route plans as failed[39m
[31m+         for (const tr of result.toolResults) {[39m
[31m+           const toolResult = tr.result as any[39m
[31m+           if (toolResult?.routePlanId) {[39m
[31m+             await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+               routePlanId: toolResult.routePlanId,[39m
[31m+               status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+               errorMessage: 'Agent did not return structured response after creating route plan',[39m
[31m+             })[39m
[31m+             break[39m
[31m+           }[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+         return {[39m
[31m+           status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+           reason: 'Agent returned unstructured response after calling tools',[39m
[31m+         }[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+       // Non-JSON response with no tool results — treat as clarification request[39m
[31m+       return {[39m
[31m+         status: 'needs_clarification',[39m
[31m+         question: result.response,[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+     // No response and no tool results — complete failure[39m
[31m+     // Update any route plan that was created before the failure[39m
[31m+     for (const tr of result.toolResults) {[39m
[31m+       const toolResult = tr.result as any[39m
[31m+       if (toolResult?.routePlanId) {[39m
[31m+         await ctx.runMutation(internal.db.routePlans.updatePlanStatus, {[39m
[31m+           routePlanId: toolResult.routePlanId,[39m
[31m+           status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+           errorMessage: 'Routing agent did not produce a route or response',[39m
[31m+         })[39m
[31m+         break[39m
[31m+       }[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+     return {[39m
[31m+       status: 'failed',[39m
[31m+       reason: 'Routing agent did not produce a route or response',[39m
[31m+     }[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // First attempt with the rider's verbatim message.[39m
[31m+   let outcome = await attempt(userMessage)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   // Guardrail: if a default origin is available, do not surface a start-origin question.[39m
[31m+   // This is not request parsing; it only corrects the agent when it ignores supplied context.[39m
[31m+   if ([39m
[31m+     outcome.status === 'needs_clarification' &&[39m
[31m+     defaultStartContext &&[39m
[31m+     isStartLocationClarification(outcome.question)[39m
[31m+   ) {[39m
[31m+     const augmentedMessage = `${userMessage}\n\n(System: the rider already has a default origin available at lat=${defaultStartContext.lat}, lng=${defaultStartContext.lng} ("${defaultStartContext.label}"). You still own the intent decision: if the rider named an explicit origin and destination, geocode those named places; otherwise use this default origin. Do NOT ask where the rider is starting.)`[39m
[31m+     outcome = await attempt(augmentedMessage)[39m
[31m+   }[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+   return outcome[39m
[31m+ }[39m
[31m+[39m

- routing_agent: plan or refine a route
- search_agent: nearby places, web search, general questions

## presentation rules
respond in 1-2 sentences, 2nd person. never expose tool names or technical details to the rider."

[32m- Expected[39m
[31m+ Received[39m

[32m- lookupRoad[39m
[31m+ You are a motorcycle ride planning assistant. Your job is to understand rider intent and pick the right specialist.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ The rider's current location is lat=37.77, lng=-122.42. Treat chat as an agent conversation: use this location as context and as the default origin for destination-only route requests. Do NOT ask "where are you starting from?" when a destination-only route can use this location. Natural-language intent still matters: "SF to Santacruze" near the Bay Area is likely a routing request, while "where is SF Bread Company" is likely a place/search request.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ## Available specialists[39m
[31m+ - routing_agent: plan or refine a route[39m
[31m+ - search_agent: nearby places, web search, general questions[39m
[31m+ - enrichment_agent: analyze the existing route (surface, weather, elevation, etc.)[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ## How to use them[39m
[31m+ - Route requests ("take me somewhere", "plan a ride to X") → routing_agent[39m
[31m+ - When intent calls for a place, common shorthand can be real place language: SF/S.F. = San Francisco, DFW = Dallas-Fort Worth, NY/NYC = New York City. Compact/misspelled Santa Cruz variants like "Santacruze" can mean Santa Cruz.[39m
[31m+ - Use context to distinguish route intent from search intent before choosing a specialist.[39m
[31m+ - Nearby places, road closures, general knowledge → search_agent[39m
[31m+ - Questions about an existing route (twisty? surface? weather?) → enrichment_agent[39m
[31m+ - Route discovery ("twisties near Asheville", "scenic routes in Oregon") → discovery_agent[39m
[31m+ - If the rider asks for multiple things, handle them one at a time — observe results before deciding the next step[39m
[31m+ - Greetings, thanks, and off-topic messages → respond directly, no specialist needed[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ## IMPORTANT: Always use your tools[39m
[31m+ When the rider asks for a route, search, question about a route, or route discovery — you MUST call the appropriate specialist tool. Do NOT respond with text instead of calling a tool. Your text response comes AFTER the tool returns results.[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ## Thinking style[39m
[31m+ When reasoning (in extended thinking / chain-of-thought), use plain rider-friendly language — your thinking is displayed as a planning indicator. Say "scenic coastal route via Big Sur" not "calling routing_agent with geocoded coordinates".[39m
[31m+[39m
[31m+ ## Presentation rules[39m
[31m+ Respond in 1-2 sentences, 2nd person. Never expose tool names or technical details to the rider.[39m

"you are a motorcycle ride planning assistant. your job is to understand rider intent and pick the right specialist.

the rider's current location is lat=37.77, lng=-122.42. treat chat as an agent conversation: use this location as context and as the default origin for destination-only route requests. do not ask \"where are you starting from?\" when a destination-only route can use this location. natural-language intent still matters: \"sf to santacruze\" near the bay area is likely a routing request, while \"where is sf bread company\" is likely a place/search request.

## available specialists
- routing_agent: plan or refine a route
- search_agent: nearby places, web search, general questions
- enrichment_agent: analyze the existing route (surface, weather, elevation, etc.)

## how to use them
- route requests (\"take me somewhere\", \"plan a ride to x\") → routing_agent
- when intent calls for a place, common shorthand can be real place language: sf/s.f. = san francisco, dfw = dallas-fort worth, ny/nyc = new york city. compact/misspelled santa cruz variants like \"santacruze\" can mean santa cruz.
- use context to distinguish route intent from search intent before choosing a specialist.
- nearby places, road closures, general knowledge → search_agent
- questions about an existing route (twisty? surface? weather?) → enrichment_agent
- route discovery (\"twisties near asheville\", \"scenic routes in oregon\") → discovery_agent
- if the rider asks for multiple things, handle them one at a time — observe results before deciding the next step
- greetings, thanks, and off-topic messages → respond directly, no specialist needed

## important: always use your tools
when the rider asks for a route, search, question about a route, or route discovery — you must call the appropriate specialist tool. do not respond with text instead of calling a tool. your text response comes after the tool returns results.

## thinking style
when reasoning (in extended thinking / chain-of-thought), use plain rider-friendly language — your thinking is displayed as a planning indicator. say \"scenic coastal route via big sur\" not \"calling routing_agent with geocoded coordinates\".

## presentation rules
respond in 1-2 sentences, 2nd person. never expose tool names or technical details to the rider."
